<span id="freeTextContainer12600097027005233070">Fast-paced and infused with JLA humor that has since become the norm when I read her books. Felt like the school aspect of the plot was a bit unrealistic (haven't read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18660669.Vampire_Academy__Vampire_Academy__1_' title='Vampire Academy (Vampire Academy #1) by Richelle Mead' rel='nofollow noopener'>Vampire Academy</a> so not sure if it was an issue in that one too) but I could be a bit biased in boarding school-related settings. I loved how she shares the same role as Seth and he doesn't get a</span>
  <span id="freeText12600097027005233070" style="display:none">Fast-paced and infused with JLA humor that has since become the norm when I read her books. Felt like the school aspect of the plot was a bit unrealistic (haven't read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18660669.Vampire_Academy__Vampire_Academy__1_" title="Vampire Academy (Vampire Academy #1) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampire Academy</a> so not sure if it was an issue in that one too) but I could be a bit biased in boarding school-related settings. Liked the main character, Alex, and Aiden, her teacher-crush. Seth was by far the favorite but he didn't have too many parts in this one. I loved how she shares the same role as Seth and he doesn't get along with Aiden, that should make things very promising for the sequel. As always, I feel like JLA's strength lies in dialogue &amp; romance, her weakness in this book was definitely the action and a bit the overall plot. Will be continuing this series as it is a light, fluffy fantasy read &amp; easy to pick up after a hectic day.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8707881602191159830"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528836426ra/25737993.gif' width='250' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>^this is to all the h8ers who don't appreciate some good YA paranormal angst</b><br/><br/>bc this shit was... good??? i've been pretty let down by a lot of YA lately <s>shatter me</s> so it was kind of refreshing to read something that was nice and entertaining.<br/><br/>now let's be clear: <b>this book isn't going to win any awards for like, achievements in literature</b> but it was FUN. we have "pure" blooded hematoi (descendent from Greek gods) and we've got, you guessed it, half bloods. both breeds fight daimons which are pure b</span>
  <span id="freeText8707881602191159830" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1528836426ra/25737993.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>^this is to all the h8ers who don't appreciate some good YA paranormal angst</b><br><br>bc this shit was... good??? i've been pretty let down by a lot of YA lately <s>shatter me</s> so it was kind of refreshing to read something that was nice and entertaining.<br><br>now let's be clear: <b>this book isn't going to win any awards for like, achievements in literature</b> but it was FUN. we have "pure" blooded hematoi (descendent from Greek gods) and we've got, you guessed it, half bloods. both breeds fight daimons which are pure blooded hematoi that have been "turned." <br><br><b>yes. this is a lot like vampire academy.<br><br>but actually, the lore is better!</b><br><br>because pure bloods and half bloods only sort of coexist. there's some inherent racism in the system. which definitely comes into play in this book; it's also a subtle thing in VA but was never fully addressed in the way that i wanted to be. i have a feeling that in future books this magical racism is gonna come into play more. <b>me likey real world issues in fantasy in paranormal.</b><br><br>that's it for plot. now the good stuff: <b>man meats</b><br><br>there's a scinty hinty of some super special <b>love geometry</b> and i'll be real clear with you: I DON'T GIVE A FUCK WHAT YOU SAY. i like love triangles. but i also think if you hate love triangles that you will still enjoy this.<br><br>also probably good to mention that our main hoe, alex, is super fun and kick ass with vulnerability. we stan a self aware queen.<br><br>if you're looking for some freaking FUN paranormal and you've been slumpy, give this a go.<br><br><b>PS thank you jess for the inadvertent recommendation, you're the realest.</b><br>-----------------------------<br><b>i'm ashamed to admit that i've started reading this...<br><br>also saddened to say that this is a less exciting, age gap free, vampire academy rip off with worse lore. but... i also have poor taste. so i'm going to continue reading it.</b></span>

<div id="review_656662901" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/656662901" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/656662901?book_show_action=true">Jul 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780983157212" href="/book/show/12689819-half-blood">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer656662901" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6435065827202053956"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_mocqncejGj1r9ccwso1_500_zpsc5213ec6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410570285i/11125365.jpg' alt=' photo tumblr_mocqncejGj1r9ccwso1_500_zpsc5213ec6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Half-Blood is book one in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. The world Jennifer has created in this series is both disturbing and amazing. This book has both intense action and sweet love. I was hooked on page one. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n263von7sn1snlqo0o1_500_zpsf397d852.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410570285i/11125366.png' alt=' photo tumblr_n263von7sn1snlqo0o1_500_zpsf397d852.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>Alexandria or Alex for short is a Half-Blood. Her mother is a pure and her father whom she never met was a mortal. Pures are like the royalty. Half-Bloods not so much. Halfs are either trained as Sentinels who hunt and kill daimons or they are forced into servitude f</span>
  <span id="freeText6435065827202053956" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_mocqncejGj1r9ccwso1_500_zpsc5213ec6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410570285i/11125365.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mocqncejGj1r9ccwso1_500_zpsc5213ec6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Half-Blood is book one in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. The world Jennifer has created in this series is both disturbing and amazing. This book has both intense action and sweet love. I was hooked on page one. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n263von7sn1snlqo0o1_500_zpsf397d852.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410570285i/11125366.png" alt=" photo tumblr_n263von7sn1snlqo0o1_500_zpsf397d852.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Alexandria or Alex for short is a Half-Blood. Her mother is a pure and her father whom she never met was a mortal. Pures are like the royalty. Half-Bloods not so much. Halfs are either trained as Sentinels who hunt and kill daimons or they are forced into servitude for the Pures. It is expressly forbidden for there EVER to be any physical relationship or emotional relationship between a Pure and a Half. Each Pure has a power of one of the elements. But their blood is also rich with aether which the daimons crave. A Half’s blood is very diluted of the aether so the daimons usually aren’t interested. Then, there is the Apollyon who is a Half but has special powers over all of the elements. There is only one Apollyon and that is Seth. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/fireonhand_zps748d943a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387761505ra/7666686.gif" alt=" photo fireonhand_zps748d943a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>First of all, I do want to say that the social standing of the Halfs in this book really bothered me. And they pretty much just accepted it. That was what they were and they will never have more. Still, though, I couldn’t help but to fall in love with Alex. She is so strong. Impulsive but strong. She has lost her mother and is doing all she can to try to catch up to the other Halfs who are training at the Covenant. The person that is training her is none other than the Pure, Aiden St. Delphi. She has fallen for him big time, even though she knows it can never be. I just love Aiden. Silent, strong, adorable Aiden. <br><br>There is something special about Alex, though. Before she found her way back to the Covenant, she was caught by a daimon and when he bit her he was amazed. <br><br><b>
  <i>“What are you?”</i>
</b><br><br>Months later when the Apollyon, Seth, showed up on campus, he repeated these words to Alex: <i>“What are you?”</i><br><br><b>
  <i>“In a matter of hours, everything had changed. Our world - my world - was no longer the same. It was too much.”</i>
</b><br><br>During those summer months Alex will experience loss, the beginnings of love, pain and strength. She is continuously deceived by those she should be able to trust. Aiden is there for her but he is still bound by his social status. Alex’s best friend, Caleb is her strongest ally throughout everything. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Do you know what your name means? Your real name - Alexandria? He smiled slowly. It means ‘Defender of Man’ in Greek.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_mzsd2sVRWy1rhvi6no1_500_zps2d2e486e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410570285i/11125367.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_mzsd2sVRWy1rhvi6no1_500_zps2d2e486e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I knew this series would be amazing and I was not disappointed. I can anticipate there is so much more coming for Alex, Aiden, Seth, and the other residents of the Covenant. I can’t wait to see what happens next.<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/ja_zps16dd050b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410368345i/11098482.jpg" alt=" photo ja_zps16dd050b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/158532643?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Avital" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Avital" href="/user/show/5151753-avital">Avital</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer158532643" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10595934815098431198">First I would like to say I've never given a book 1 star, because I think that just the dedication of an author earns him at list 2 stars. The second thing is that I think that's the longest review I've ever wrote. It says something.<br/><br/>This book doesn't deserve rating at all. Because it was a perfect copy of Vampire Academy series. And not in a good way.<br/>I'm utterly disappointed and upset with Jennifer L. Armentrout. How can she do that? How did the publishers let her publish a book that is a copy o</span>
  <span id="freeText10595934815098431198" style="display:none">First I would like to say I've never given a book 1 star, because I think that just the dedication of an author earns him at list 2 stars. The second thing is that I think that's the longest review I've ever wrote. It says something.<br /><br />This book doesn't deserve rating at all. Because it was a perfect copy of Vampire Academy series. And not in a good way.<br />I'm utterly disappointed and upset with Jennifer L. Armentrout. How can she do that? How did the publishers let her publish a book that is a copy of another?<br /><br />First of all, the main idea. Daimons? Half-bloods? Pures? It equals Strigoi, Damphirs and Moroi.<br />Once a Pure drinks the Aether (blood) from another, it becomes a monster, a Daimon. It's just like vampires.<br /><br />The plot begins with Alex who is returning to the Covenant (The Academy) after a long time. She needs to catch up with her training, to be a Guardian - Oops, a Sentinel one day and kill Strigoi - ah, Daimons. And of course no one agrees to give her private training, except for the hot Sentinel (Guardian) Aiden.<br /><br />Just like with Dimitri in VA.<br /><br />From then the plot focuses on the relationship of Alex and Aiden and her training.<br /><br />Some of the scenes with Alex and Aiden were just like with Rose and Dimitri that I really became furious. Aiden treating Alex with her injury just like Dimitri did Rose, Aiden preaching Alex about her behavior like Dimitri did.<br /><br />And the characters!<br />Alex=Rose.<br />Aiden=Dimitri.<br />Lea=Mia.<br />Caleb=Mason.<br />Deacon=Adrian.<br /><br />And I'm sure there's more.<br /><br />And the ending?? Alex being kidnapped just like in book 2 in VA series. <br /><br />I tried to give this book a chance when I started reading it and noticed all the similarities because I thought- NO WAY IS SHE COPYING EVERY WORD AND EVERY SCENE!<br /><br />But she did. And it's just a shame.</span>

  <b>"Always beware of the one who needs you. <br>There is always a want behind a need, you see.”</b>

Alex) Andros</b> (17 y/o) is just like Rose—the stubborn and reckless girl we all know and love (at least I think we do xD). Here, they live in a world of where the Greek Gods are real and you're either a pure-blood or half-blood (basically like Moroi or Dhampir). <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1601950289i/30198748.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Alex</b> is of course, a half-blood and with that, they have their own school, the <b>Covenant</b>, for half-bloods like her to train to become Sentinels or Guards and protect the pure-bloods from monsters gone evil—<b>the <s>Strigoi</s> Daimons</b>. <div id="review_173163750" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/173163750" />
    <a title="MISS VAIN" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4335141-miss-vain"><img alt="MISS VAIN" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312749379p2/4335141.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/173163750?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="MISS VAIN" class="user" itemprop="url" name="MISS VAIN" href="/user/show/4335141-miss-vain">MISS VAIN</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Copy &amp; paste fans!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4335141-miss-vain?shelf=series-that-i-m-obsessed-with">series-that-i-m-obsessed-with</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4335141-miss-vain?shelf=jennifer-l-armentrout">jennifer-l-armentrout</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer173163750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2300580281375028025"><b> "There's nothing like a bunch of catty teenagers who could either kick your ass halfway across the country or set you on fire with a mere thought. <br/><br/>That alone changed who people picked fights with or became friends with. <br/>And at the end of the day, it was always good to have a Firestarter in your back pocket." </b> <br/><br/>Okay soooo As a HUGE Vampire Academy fan please allow me to adress the whole "It's just like V.A. Issue"..... Well it did have several moments especially in the beginning as well as the co</span>
  <span id="freeText2300580281375028025" style="display:none"><b> "There's nothing like a bunch of catty teenagers who could either kick your ass halfway across the country or set you on fire with a mere thought. <br /><br />That alone changed who people picked fights with or became friends with. <br />And at the end of the day, it was always good to have a Firestarter in your back pocket." </b> <br /><br />Okay soooo As a HUGE Vampire Academy fan please allow me to adress the whole "It's just like V.A. Issue"..... Well it did have several moments especially in the beginning as well as the concept that held an uncanny resemblance to Vampire Academy, there's no denying that, however keep reading because <b>Half-Blood</b> transforms into something unique and desirable that will capture the hearts of their own fans. In Half-Blood the premise revolves around mythical creatures which I'm finding very intriguing at this moment. <br /><br />Meet Alexandria, or more preferably known as <b>Alex</b>, she's smart, witty, fascinating, sarcastic, irresponsible, and basically thinks she's "bad-ass" like every other seventeen year old and she charmed me from page one. She's considered a <b>Half-Blood</b>; with her father a mundane human and her mother a <b>Hematoi</b> a very powerful race of Pure-Bloods, a product of the Greeks shacking up after the demigods died. She finds herself back at the Covenant living on Deity Island after her mom succumbed to an attack by force from a group of Daimons. <br /><br /><b> "She was everything to me!" I jumped to my feet. "She did nothing but think of me. What happened to her was horrific---'tragic' is for people who die in car wrecks!" </b><br /><br /><b>Daimons</b> are basically the Strigoi of this series, but they drink blood from Pures and Half to obtain the Aether carried in their bloodstream. If you can't get past the Vampire Academy similarities stop now, but if you can you're in for an awesome new series because it takes us readers on an entirely different ride than Vampire Academy. It's equally emotionally charged but look put because the plot is uniquely heartbreaking, breathtaking, and exciting!!!!:-)<br /><br /><b>"Just picture me as the enemy Alexandria."<br /><br />Oh that won't be too hard, Dean Andros." <br /><br /><i>I raised my hands and motioned him forward. I was a total badass."</i> </b><br /><br />Alex becomes determined to become a Sentinel guard to protect others from the tragic incident with the Daimons that has changed her life forever. In many ways she's wise beyond her seventeen years and at times she's just a struggling teenager with fantasies of love and immeasurable dreams. <br /><br /><br />Her best friend <b>Caleb</b> was an extremely desirable best friend to have and he was hilarious!!! I found him extremely likable and a very reliable friend to Alex. What I love most is that they both supportive friends and that just it; they're platonic friends with no desire of a relationship, a productive example once again that males and females can be just friends. I look forward to more of Caleb throughout this series. <br /><br /><b> <i>Caleb stood up as I walked into the living room.</i>"You look hot."<i>I scrunched up my face.</i>"You think this is hot?"<i>He laughed as he turned toward the door.</i>"No"</b><br /><br /><br />Then there's the sexy <b>Aiden</b> St. Delfi, a Full Blood also referred to as <b>Hematoi</b>; he's fiercely responsible and dedicated to training Alex to becoming a powerful Sentinel. He also unbeknownst to himself has been in possesion of the key to Alex's heart for the past three years. Quickly he becomes her confidant, mentor, and masculine shoulder to cry on. He proves himself crushworthy <s>Swoon</s> along the way and you cannot help but encourage the budding relationship between Alex and Aiden because he's loyal, trustworthy, strong, and cares about Alex's well being above his own. When Aiden St. isn't training his forbidden crush Alex he is carrying out the parental figure with his alcoholic abusing fun loving, promiscuous brother Deacon and each and every scene he's in was a mixture of fun and rebellion.<br /><br />But wait because the list of lustworthy males is still in abundance because I can't seem to get dangerously gifted <b>Seth</b> The <b>Apollyon</b> out of my thoughts, especially since he is also described as being inhumanely gorgeous by Alex. <br /><br /><b> "I knew you were here. Not you so to speak. But I knew someone---someone different. I felt it outside, before I entered the lobby. It was like a magnetic pull. I zeroed in on you immediately. That has never happened before." <br /><br /><i> he unfolded his arms to reach for me. I pulled back. There were a multitude of reasons why I didn't want him to touch me. Alarmed that he was actually going to, </i><br /><br /><i> I blurted out the first thing that came to my mind.</i> <br /><br /><blockquote> "I saw your tattoos."</blockquote><br /><br /><i> Seth froze. Hell he no longer looked like he wanted to touch me, or be in the same zip code as me. </i> </b><br /><br />The Apollyon is a unique and rare anomaly amongst the half bloods. As an Apollyon he has mastered every element at a Full Blood's disposal such as <i>Air, Water, Fire, as well as Earth Spells and Compulsions</i> all at once and his blood is merely classified as a half blood. Often he's feared and revered amongst his kind as almost a deity as he is all powerful and has no limitations on what powers are at his disposal. He holds plenty of mystery as well as inherited gifts that enables him to be more powerful than even the purest of Hematoi. There's something about a mystically charismatic character with a bit of a feisty naughty boy quality that captures my attention and mesmerizes me to <i>no</i> end.<br /><br /><br /><br />For those readers like myself that need plenty of males to gush about in not only do we get funny lovable Caleb, but we get Fiercely responsible Aiden, irresponsible Deacon and mysterious Seth. <br /><br />I can already see that this premiere series by <b>Jennifer L. Armentrout</b> will be on my favorites list. This book was amazing and with all of it's plot twists and turns, I can't even imagine what is in store for us readers in <b>Pure Blood</b> next year. <br /><br /><br />Alex begins this journey as a rebellious adolescent, that unfortunately has to grow up when she is faced with the task of killing someone she loves in a technique of self preservation. <br /><br /><b><i>What was I supposed to do? Kill her, Run from her. Save her somehow?</i> </b><br /><br />She endures all this angst while enjoying a taste of love, experiencing immeasurable pain, fortunately she has the comforting embrace of a loyal and devoted friend. <br /><br />Alex receives an electrifying revelation that will change her life forever as a predestined future set forth by the gods before her. I'm <s>Obsessed</s> excited to find out how this revelation into her bloodline is carried out with this series and a certain someone.<br /><br />I can't say enough wonderfully awesome things about this book! I <b> loved, loved, loved it!!!</b><br /><br />For all of you readers that enjoy an exciting page turner this is the book for you. <br /><br /><br /><b> <blockquote> "This cannot be happening."</blockquote><br /><i>He looked up his eyes glowed in the darkness. The bewildered look faded replaced by anger.</i><br /><br /><blockquote>"We're going to die."</blockquote> </b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />Like what you see here, check out more of my reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://missvainsparanormalfantasy.com/">http://missvainsparanormalfantasy.com/</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2300580281375028025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/507035833" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/507035833?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780983157212" href="/book/show/12689819-half-blood">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jacqueline's Reads by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/16453761-tricia-santos">Tricia  Santos</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=6-stars-top-favorites">6-stars-top-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer507035833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3662115160803205729"><b>FIVE FUN FACTS about JENNIFER L. ARMENTROUT + Book Signing Photos - > <a href='http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/11/half-blood-covenant-1-jennifer-l.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a></b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/G4Atv5y' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385092694i/7064231._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>6 FUCK ME HARD (OR JUST RUB UPON ME) AIDEN STARS</b><br/><br/>It’s not secret I am a Jennifer L. Armentrout (J.Lynn) fan. Yes, I have a girl crush list (just like a book boyfriend list) and she is an author that is on there. So, with my mini me (that’s my reading buddy, I call her mini me, b/c she’s ten years younger than me and reminds me of me ten years ago) told me to read Half-Blood, I said, well what the heck.<br/><br/>Oh my god, where h</span>
  <span id="freeText3662115160803205729" style="display:none"><b>FIVE FUN FACTS about JENNIFER L. ARMENTROUT + Book Signing Photos - &gt; <a href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/11/half-blood-covenant-1-jennifer-l.html" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/G4Atv5y" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385092694i/7064231._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>6 FUCK ME HARD (OR JUST RUB UPON ME) AIDEN STARS</b><br><br>It’s not secret I am a Jennifer L. Armentrout (J.Lynn) fan. Yes, I have a girl crush list (just like a book boyfriend list) and she is an author that is on there. So, with my mini me (that’s my reading buddy, I call her mini me, b/c she’s ten years younger than me and reminds me of me ten years ago) told me to read Half-Blood, I said, well what the heck.<br><br>Oh my god, where have I been and I can’t believe I didn’t pick up the Covenant series sooner! I love the Lux series, but book 1, Half-Blood, oh no comparison.<br><br><b>I fucking gobble this shit up and real good! (I know that didn’t make sense, but it was the only way I could convey my feelings)</b><br><br>Alex (Alexandria) is a Half-Blood and Aiden is a Pure (full-blood). Alex ran away from the Covenant (a school) for three years and finally came back, b/c her mother died. Aiden is in charge of training Alex to get her up to speed, so when school starts Alex isn’t so far behind.<br><br>Okay, that summary is just a TIP of what you will be reading. First off, the whole half-blood, pure, daimon, Sentinel is all confusing to me, but eventually you get the hang of it and all that stuff is just story, what really did it was the writing style. Oh how I love Armentrout’s writing, how can you write a YA book with that much wonderful sexual tension? I do not know but she does it.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/qq4oAzg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385092694i/7064232.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I love Alex, she’s strong, feisty and never really irrational. I want to be her and you do feel for her. It’s sometimes hard for me to sympathize with young Heroines or Heroines in YA paranormal reads, but I completely was in tune with Alex. So yes, I could imagine myself as a seventeen year old Half-Blood. Oh Aiden, how much I love him. Sigh, swoon, major book boyfriend. Half-Blood reminded me a lot like Divergent, the whole older Hero training the young Heroine thing just does it for me. It’s cute, it’s adorable and you will be glued reading the pages. <br><br>There’s tension from the students, there’s tension from external forces and there’s tension from the school, but it’s NEVER annoying. It’s just the right amount to get you going. The majority of the story is Alex and Aiden, THANK YOU! Yes, there’s back story and side characters, but I love reads where it’s mainly about the Hero and Heroine.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/NM0jySx" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385092694i/7064233._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>BUT do not be fooled, this is no boring read and there’s plenty of twists and turns! I was like Oh my god until the last second and you will too.<br><br>If you aren’t a huge fan of YA paranormal reads, I just think you aren’t picking up the right books. I get you, the whole super natural stuff, is like huh? BUT believe me, if it’s written well, you will definitely keep these types of books on your shelf. Try Half-Blood, you will be a fan!<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9680718.Half_Blood__Covenant___1_" title="Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1311865840s/9680718.jpg" alt="Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0983157200/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=0983157200&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3662115160803205729" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_608316946" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/608316946" />
    <a title="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies"><img alt="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1500999223p2/4527753.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/608316946?book_show_action=true">May 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies" href="/user/show/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies">Khanh, first of her name, mother of bunnies</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=b-word-heroine">b-word-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=boarding-school">boarding-school</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4527753-khanh-first-of-her-name-mother-of-bunnies?shelf=nice-authors">nice-authors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer608316946" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5222813970569749845">I might have rated this book higher had I read this before Richelle Mead's <i>Vampire Academy</i> series. As it stands, the characters and the plot all feels like a very watered down version of VA. I couldn't help comparing one character to the next, and they all felt lacking. The premise is slightly different, but the boarding school setting, the reviled and necessary half-bloods, the evil daimons/strigoi, all felt rehashed, and not in a good way.<br/><br/>Alex is Rose, without the spunk, with more slut-shaming</span>
  <span id="freeText5222813970569749845" style="display:none">I might have rated this book higher had I read this before Richelle Mead's <i>Vampire Academy</i> series. As it stands, the characters and the plot all feels like a very watered down version of VA. I couldn't help comparing one character to the next, and they all felt lacking. The premise is slightly different, but the boarding school setting, the reviled and necessary half-bloods, the evil daimons/strigoi, all felt rehashed, and not in a good way.<br /><br />Alex is Rose, without the spunk, with more slut-shaming (does she really need to repeatedly call her nemesis Lea a skank? Is it necessary to mention that Lea is probably promiscuous?). Her actions are more impulsive than rational. While Rose is literally, kick-ass, Alex is relatively weak, and her wins versus the daimons seemed more coincidental than from purely skill. Like Rose, Alex has been on the run for awhile, but it feels like she lacks the common sense to survive on her own.<br /><br />While Rose is spunky and impulsive, she has the good sense to keep it under control when it matters most, whereas Alex just feels the need to be contrary just for the sake of pissing people off, even when she is endangering her whole future. When your options are entering in a lifelong sentence of mindless servitude or being a more or less respected Sentinel, any person with common sense would try to behave and not get into further trouble. Not Alex. She is smart-mouthed and just a jerk in general, even admitting it herself.<br /><br />There is the love interest, Aiden, a watered-down version of Dimitri. Caleb, the lesser version of Christian. The almighty Seth is the only one of whom I can't find a clear-cut double in Vampire Academy, but he's not altogether likeable yet.<br /><br />It seems as if all of Alex's companions and closer friends are male. I'm really smelling a Mary Sue here, but I'll continue on with the series to see if that's the case.<br /><br />I do like the incorporation of mythology. Whereas in some other series I've read like <i>Mythos Academy</i>, the living gods and goddesses do not get involved in the characters of their creation, whereas here they actually do take a part in monitoring their descendants. I enjoy the bits of lore, and I hope that will be fleshed out in the books to come.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5222813970569749845" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4165051397342513112">This book is amazing! Fans of VAMPIRE ACADEMY will love it. The main character, Alex, has a wonderfully edgy, sarcastic voice, and she's simultaneously strong and vulnerable. I pulled this query out of the slush pile and read the manuscript in a day--I couldn't put it down! Put this on your "to-read" list; you won't be disappointed! </span>

<div id="review_137448000" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/137448000" />
    <a title="Ceitidh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3850693-ceitidh"><img alt="Ceitidh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469631051p2/3850693.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/137448000?book_show_action=true">Dec 30, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ceitidh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ceitidh" href="/user/show/3850693-ceitidh">Ceitidh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3850693-ceitidh?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3850693-ceitidh?shelf=not-finished">not-finished</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer137448000" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer691932067722354792">Okay, a few people has asked me why I only gave 1 cheap star to this book that seems to be a favorite of so many. So, I decided to explain how I feel towards this book with the following points.<br/><br/>But first, I am sorry in advance if I offend a fan of this series. I know it hurts when someone talks crap about a book you love and I know this book has tones of fans but SORRY!<br/><br/>So here I go!<br/><br/>1. I got almost halfway through the book. I read like 45% of it and I couldn't keep reading. So yes, I didnt' finis</span>
  <span id="freeText691932067722354792" style="display:none">Okay, a few people has asked me why I only gave 1 cheap star to this book that seems to be a favorite of so many. So, I decided to explain how I feel towards this book with the following points.<br /><br />But first, I am sorry in advance if I offend a fan of this series. I know it hurts when someone talks crap about a book you love and I know this book has tones of fans but SORRY!<br /><br />So here I go!<br /><br />1. I got almost halfway through the book. I read like 45% of it and I couldn't keep reading. So yes, I didnt' finish it. It's not that is a bad book, or that the writing sucked (my own writing actually sucks big time so I never judge about that aspect) but I think is pretty much a big copy of Vampire Academy.<br />I know, WOW! big heavy words, but if you read Vampire Academy then you'll immediately notice the striking similarities between both books. And by striking similarities I mean general plot, characters, species, romance,even dialogues! I remember Aiden told something about the daggers to Alex (Aiden is training Alex under pretty much the same circumstances as Dimitri is training Rose) something like "you haven't earned the right to use one of those" (He said this when Alex wanted to grab one of the dagger) Well, something very similar happened in Vampire Academy) and the similarities continue and are endless! (and notice that I didn't even finished the book. I just got halfway through it and that was enough for me to feel like I was reading a complete Vampire Academy rip-off. Hopefully thing changed by the end of the book and things turned out to be Armentrout's own ideas (I really hoped that). However, I have been talking with a few friends and it happens that, according to them, that's not the case. (that is the opinion from people who did finish the book, just so you know)<br /><br />2. I feel like the author tried to re-write Vampire Academy on her own way (but not really, she just changed the names and places) and then oops! it happened she sold it and got published. I still wonder, how that even happened? O_o?? I knew there were similarities between VA and this book but... aren't they too many? hmmmmmm... <br /><br />3. I cannot like a book I felt uncomfortable reading and for respect to Richelle Mead, I coudln't keep turning this book's pages without feeling like crap for her. And that's why I willingly stopped reading this book. Thanks LORD I didnt buy it but borrowed it from a friend! if not, I would have burned it already.<br /><br />I totally understand when books (or whatever) have similarities. That's totally fine. Originality is impossible and everything comes from something else. That's what sources and inspiration are for. But well... this is not the case.<br /><br />There you have it my dear fellow readers. You may actually enjoy this book if you have never read Vampire Academy. Otherwise, it may feel repetitive, predictable and even offensive! (it was in my case)<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="691932067722354792" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/288856622" />
    <a title="Booknut" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6917862-booknut"><img alt="Booknut" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1411194489p2/6917862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/288856622?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Booknut" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Booknut" href="/user/show/6917862-booknut">Booknut</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6917862-booknut?shelf=can-t-get-enough-of">can-t-get-enough-of</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer288856622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12638008199456466855"><u>Re-read 30/9/13</u>:<br/><br/>Re-reading this book was like visiting an old friend with a <i>great</i> sense of humour! I fell in love with this series all over again from the very first page - the tale of Alex, the kickass halfblood heroine, and her journey, one that I will never, ever tire of :)<br/><br/><u>Original Review</u><br/><br/><i>"It was him - Aiden St.Delphi."</i><br/><br/>As soon as I read that I was all like, "Oooooh yeah. She's got it baaaaaad." But then I read about how pures and halfs can't be together and I was all:<br/><a target='_blank' title='ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting' href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/850/wowb.gif/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371531ra/724640.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://imageshack.us' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/>Shit. Is. Going. To. G</span>
  <span id="freeText12638008199456466855" style="display:none"><u>Re-read 30/9/13</u>:<br><br>Re-reading this book was like visiting an old friend with a <i>great</i> sense of humour! I fell in love with this series all over again from the very first page - the tale of Alex, the kickass halfblood heroine, and her journey, one that I will never, ever tire of :)<br><br><u>Original Review</u><br><br><i>"It was him - Aiden St.Delphi."</i><br><br>As soon as I read that I was all like, "Oooooh yeah. She's got it baaaaaad." But then I read about how pures and halfs can't be together and I was all:<br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/850/wowb.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371531ra/724640.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br>Shit. Is. Going. To. Go. Down.<br><br>What really annoyed me was that no one seemed to have any faith in her. I mean - hello?! The girl survived on her own and killed two daimons, plus she saw her mum die. I think I wasn't the only annoyed one - Alexandria was pretty upset too. But Aiden's like "No one here is your enemy, Alex, it's all in your head - I'm sure they all want to come over and have a tea party later on."<br><a target="_blank" title="ImageShack - Image And Video Hosting" href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/831/ohk.gif/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380371531ra/724641.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://imageshack.us" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br>Sure, buddy... <i>sure</i> .<br><br>Kickass - with tonnes of action, a brilliant new world and Armentrout's signature humour - this book is epic and is a definite must-read.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12638008199456466855" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_219273891" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/219273891" />
    <a title="Sabrina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5771244-sabrina"><img alt="Sabrina" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/219273891?book_show_action=true">Oct 05, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sabrina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sabrina" href="/user/show/5771244-sabrina">Sabrina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780983157212" href="/book/show/12689819-half-blood">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people who liked the Vampire Academy series and would like to read the same thing over and over</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5771244-sabrina?shelf=series-abandoned">series-abandoned</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer219273891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12379925256164188630">I just got into the first few pages and the "WTF counter" was already exploding.<br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/what%20gifs/ChristineFerrara/GIFs/Minion-What.gif?o=32' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360635ra/711529.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I get it that you'd like to write a book but don't have anything new to say.<br/>I get it that you are unsure and feel more secure using elements already proven successful.<br/>I get it that you REALLY liked the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/42114-vampire-academy' rel='nofollow noopener'>Vampire Academy series</a>.<br/>I don't think you have to be completely original to write a (good) book: you are allowed to pick ideas here and there.<br/><br/>But.<br/><br/>SERIOUSLY.<br/><br/>COME ON.</span>
  <span id="freeText12379925256164188630" style="display:none">I just got into the first few pages and the "WTF counter" was already exploding.<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/what%20gifs/ChristineFerrara/GIFs/Minion-What.gif?o=32" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380360635ra/711529.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I get it that you'd like to write a book but don't have anything new to say.<br>I get it that you are unsure and feel more secure using elements already proven successful.<br>I get it that you REALLY liked the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/42114-vampire-academy" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampire Academy series</a>.<br>I don't think you have to be completely original to write a (good) book: you are allowed to pick ideas here and there.<br><br>But.<br><br>SERIOUSLY.<br><br>COME ON.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12379925256164188630" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OwN9m+Kxi/t+NE+lySS6TKfcy6x1+N/3ZBNzQjRvwKIwsc8VJkWNJ8RrVc7N9311T21hgs7aZg0cvfym1BUX9Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('te6qUNMPqi9FmrLNmY8alatVnMNvNHt7Dk19/z6L6+2+XBjeF/us8//FqKadXN2sQ+Q27dQWwoF24/Ib3vE8ug==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText1437902470413227633" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
